# Items

Like most Pokémon games, Pokémon Pokopia has a myriad of items including Materials and cosmetic items you can use to decaorate the islands and houses throughout the game. This page is to list all the items and will add their locations over time as we figure exact locations out.

Details

**Developer:**

[GAME FREAK](https://serebii.net/pokemon/companies/gamefreak.shtml)

[Koei Tecmo](https://serebii.net/pokemon/companies/koeitecmo.shtml)

**Genre:**

Life Simulation

**Players:**

1-4
